  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_e8de29b3-a183-4655-8950-51384a7ce086'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2310268348" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18288793787221504959"><b>Finale</b><br/>The Ghost Hunter is the final book of the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness and will ultimately bring Torak's quest to an end. In this final book, Torak, Renn and Wolf meet the most powerful of the Soul Eaters - Eostra. Each will face grief, doubts, hardships and exhaustion in throwing every once of their energy and ability at this final battle. The prize is to turn their lands back from the evil abyss they all face. Will they all survive??<br/><br/>The 6 book series written by Michelle Paver should be</span>
  <span id="freeText18288793787221504959" style="display:none"><b>Finale</b><br />The Ghost Hunter is the final book of the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness and will ultimately bring Torak's quest to an end. In this final book, Torak, Renn and Wolf meet the most powerful of the Soul Eaters - Eostra. Each will face grief, doubts, hardships and exhaustion in throwing every once of their energy and ability at this final battle. The prize is to turn their lands back from the evil abyss they all face. Will they all survive??<br /><br />The 6 book series written by Michelle Paver should be made into a television series it's so good. The setting is thrilling, being based 6 thousand years ago when the world was still heavily forested. The descriptions of the ancient forests are excellent and there's still a feeling of the Earth rebuilding after the last ice age. The stories are a great adventure of good versus evil, of supernatural and mythical backdrops, and of friendships and commitments to put your life on the line to protect those you love. It is aimed at an older child / younger adult audience so the dialogue and narrative can be taken at face value. I did enjoy sharing these stories with my children and did it very willingly.</span>

  <span id="freeText15432795505782883628" style="display:none">Reading the last page of this book left me with such emotion, especially since the first time I picked up the first book was...quite sometime ago.<br /><br />The final book did not let me down as much as other final books have. <div id="review_3035259766" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3035259766" />
    <a title="Thomas" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/63824806-thomas"><img alt="Thomas" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484326813p2/63824806.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3035259766?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Thomas" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Thomas" href="/user/show/63824806-thomas">Thomas</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer3035259766&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3035259766" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9695024464666020993">I started rereading this series back in 2018 because it is one of my all time favourites. Having now finished the original 6 books, I can say that I am very happy with my experience and looking forward to reading 3 more books set in this world.<br/><br/>Ghost Hunter was the final novel in the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness and I thought Michelle Paver delivered an absolutely spectacular finale. I think it is one of the best in the series, outranked only by Wolf Brother, because this was the novel that int</span>
  <span id="freeText9695024464666020993" style="display:none">I started rereading this series back in 2018 because it is one of my all time favourites. Having now finished the original 6 books, I can say that I am very happy with my experience and looking forward to reading 3 more books set in this world.<br /><br />Ghost Hunter was the final novel in the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness and I thought Michelle Paver delivered an absolutely spectacular finale. I think it is one of the best in the series, outranked only by Wolf Brother, because this was the novel that introduced Torak’s world so brilliantly to begin with.<br /><br />Having defeated Thiazzi in Oathbreaker, Torak must now face the deadliest Soul Eater of them all, Eostra, the Eagle Owl Mage. Eostra holds the forest in a grip of fear with demons and the dead at her command. Torak and Wolf need every ounce of skill and luck they possess to defeat her. <br /><br />As with every book she has written in this series, Paver’s writing style is flawless when it comes to describing the nature of the ancient world. You truly feel drawn into a setting that is incredibly rich and detailed.<br /><br />I feel that Ghost Hunter was a satisfying conclusion to the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness and I am pleased to give the novel 5 stars. I would recommend the whole series to any adult or teenager that enjoys the fantasy genre. I look forward to reading more adventures in this world when I start reading Viper’s Daughter in the near future.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9695024464666020993" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_107440324" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/107440324" />
    <a title="Phoebe" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2807810-phoebe"><img alt="Phoebe" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596327344p2/2807810.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/107440324?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Phoebe" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Phoebe" href="/user/show/2807810-phoebe">Phoebe</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780060728403" href="/book/show/7217246-ghost-hunter-chronicles-of-ancient-darkness-6">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer107440324" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16605865844181747824">Sadly, the final volume in this truly great series. Unnatural winter and sickness, sent by Eostra, the scary Eagle Owl Mage, are killing the tribes, and Torak realizes he must venture out and fight Eostra, who seeks Torak, the last Soul Eater, to gain ultimate power. Compelling, creepy, and just plain good storytelling. Recommended for adventure fans, unique for its post-Ice Age, pre-farming time setting. Paver did meticulous research and traveled extensively to write her books.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2790369045" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2790369045" />
    <a title="Jennie Louwes" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/89985522-jennie-louwes"><img alt="Jennie Louwes" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1584340118p2/89985522.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2790369045?book_show_action=true">Apr 23, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennie Louwes" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennie Louwes" href="/user/show/89985522-jennie-louwes">Jennie Louwes</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780060728403" href="/book/show/7217246-ghost-hunter-chronicles-of-ancient-darkness-6">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2790369045" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8565132987912178109">"Ghost Hunter", the final installment of "The Chronicles of Ancient Darkness", does not disappoint! One cliffhanger after another both figuratively and literally. From the first page to the last your heart rate quickens as you rush towards the inevitable finale.<br/><br/>The book opens with buds of happiness that are blossoming into full on joy; but, it doesn't last. Abruptly things change with such suddenness that it brought tears to my 11 year old boy-child's eyes. Thus begins the roller-coaster of even</span>
  <span id="freeText8565132987912178109" style="display:none">"Ghost Hunter", the final installment of "The Chronicles of Ancient Darkness", does not disappoint! One cliffhanger after another both figuratively and literally. From the first page to the last your heart rate quickens as you rush towards the inevitable finale.<br /><br />The book opens with buds of happiness that are blossoming into full on joy; but, it doesn't last. Abruptly things change with such suddenness that it brought tears to my 11 year old boy-child's eyes. Thus begins the roller-coaster of events within the "Ghost Hunter". <br /><br />The addition of a character named "Dark" is a wonderful one. His name a brilliant oxymoron that's simple and yet of great depth; he wears his name well.<br /><br />The culmination of events is gratifying. Though it's incredibly hard to say, "goodbye" to such wonderful, literary friends. Of course, better to see those you've come to love walking hand-in-hand towards the sunset than being separated by death, no? <br /><br />The way in which things end allows you to believe in a happily ever after that's eternal. That's what story does when it doesn't culminate with "The End". <br /><br />The ending, like the beginning, is enough to spark tearfilled eyes; but, this time the tears are pure joy.<br /><br />Thank you, Michelle Paver, for sharing your life's experiences through story with us. Extraordinary moments have been a part of your life; therefore, it's the extrodinary you have managed to weave within "The Chronicles of Ancient Darkness". Thank you for sharing your cast of characters and for making the journey so real and relevant. <br /><br />It's bittersweet to now say, "adieu", thank goodness you've written other books too! May you always find there's a place for you with an eager audience waiting.<br /><br />Written with utmost sincerity,<br /><br />Jennie Louwes</span>
  <a data-text-id="8565132987912178109" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1468088467" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1468088467" />
    <a title="Big Pete" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47746222-big-pete"><img alt="Big Pete" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1469016966p2/47746222.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1468088467?book_show_action=true">Dec 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Big Pete" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Big Pete" href="/user/show/47746222-big-pete">Big Pete</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1468088467" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4886872565618422607">The tale that began with <i>Wolf Brother</i> comes full circle with <i>Ghost Hunter</i>. I first read this book in (somewhat appropriately) the winter of 2010. It has not lost its genius since. Torak, Renn, Wolf and Fin-Kedinn have come a long way from who they once were. They are all much older, but where the younger members of the cast have matured, Fin-Kedinn is beginning to feel the bite of old age. <br/>Grey moths are pervading the pre-winter Forest, bringing foul dreams to the clans. Torak, though worried, c</span>
  <span id="freeText4886872565618422607" style="display:none">The tale that began with <i>Wolf Brother</i> comes full circle with <i>Ghost Hunter</i>. I first read this book in (somewhat appropriately) the winter of 2010. It has not lost its genius since. Torak, Renn, Wolf and Fin-Kedinn have come a long way from who they once were. They are all much older, but where the younger members of the cast have matured, Fin-Kedinn is beginning to feel the bite of old age. <br />Grey moths are pervading the pre-winter Forest, bringing foul dreams to the clans. Torak, though worried, can do little about this new menace. One night, as he sits alone, watching the Raven Clan as they sleep, Torak hears a voice coming from the trees, soft and pleading. He investigates, and sees the shade of his father, former Soul-Eater and the Wolf Mage; killed by a monstrous bear some months past.<br />He strikes out into the wilderness, but his journey is far from uneventful. Tragedy strikes, and Wolf's family is shattered almost irreparably.<br />Torak and Renn head north to the Mountain of Ghosts, where Eostra, Eagle Owl Mage and last of the Soul-Eaters sets in motion a plan that will bring the whole of the Forest and the North under her sway...<br /><i>Ghost Hunter</i> is by turns, reserved, intense, funny, melancholic, joyous, eerie and heart-breaking. The characters (already well-rounded and interesting) grow even more, and we see a return of some old battlers I thought we'd never see again. The new character Dark is particularly of note, a sad, lost recluse who nonetheless finds a sense of kinship with Torak and Renn. We learn much more about the culture and life of the clans, and it is, as always, fascinating.<br /><br /><i>Ghost Hunter</i> is a triumphant return to form for Paver, and one of her best novels. You don't want the series to end, but the ending is more than satisfying. This is one of the best novels in the series, perhaps even better than the brilliant <i>Soul Eater</i> </span>
  <a data-text-id="4886872565618422607" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_127890705" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/127890705" />
    <a title="Evan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4285429-evan"><img alt="Evan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1317740206p2/4285429.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/127890705?book_show_action=true">Oct 25, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Evan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Evan" href="/user/show/4285429-evan">Evan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4285429-evan?shelf=6th-grade">6th-grade</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer127890705&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer127890705" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17348216667295458406"><br/>Six thousand years ago in the forests of Europe where people live in clans, evil threatens the lands. The last living soul eater, Eostra, the Eagle Owl Mage sends a shadow sickness to the clans. Orphaned teenage boy, Torak, is the one to stop the last and final Soul Eater from killing all life in the forest. Torak is not alone in his journey to the Mountain of Ghosts. His companions are Wolf, a wolf who Torak can speak to using wolf talk, and Renn, a mage in training for magic from the Raven Cla</span>
  <span id="freeText17348216667295458406" style="display:none"><br />Six thousand years ago in the forests of Europe where people live in clans, evil threatens the lands. The last living soul eater, Eostra, the Eagle Owl Mage sends a shadow sickness to the clans. Orphaned teenage boy, Torak, is the one to stop the last and final Soul Eater from killing all life in the forest. Torak is not alone in his journey to the Mountain of Ghosts. His companions are Wolf, a wolf who Torak can speak to using wolf talk, and Renn, a mage in training for magic from the Raven Clan. Torak possesses an ability that is very rare--he is a spirit walker which means he can move into an animal’s mind for a short period of time and control them. Torak’s journey to the Mountain of Ghosts causes him to see his father as a ghost being summoned along with the dead Soul Eaters by Eostra. See what happens when Torak sees his father again. This will be Torak’s final battle against evil and will he survive?<br /><br />This is the final book in the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness series. This book ties up the series with a “5 star” ending to Torak’s journey. I liked that throughout Ghost Hunter, the author, Michelle Paver, really keeps your attention with lots of action. She switches characters and you read what is going on in Wolf's mind or Renn's mind. If you are eager to learn about the shocking decision that Torak makes then this is the right book for you!</span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText3355418984432536961" style="display:none">|3.5 Stars|<br /><br />Ladies and gentlemen, I am <i> finally </i> done with the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness. This is a series I started as a child, read books one and two and <i> maybe </i> three, started reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3389.Stephen_King" title="Stephen King" rel="nofollow noopener">Stephen King</a> and thus abandoned everything in the children's library except for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/27498.Erin_Hunter" title="Erin Hunter" rel="nofollow noopener">Erin Hunter</a>. A few years ago, I bought the entire series off of BookOutlet and man, I am finally done.<br /><br />Let's get this straight--I loved the first two books. I loved them as a kid, and I did really enjoy them as an adult. But man, as this series went on, it <i> dragged </i>. Books four and five nearly killed me. It's not like, Lorien Legacies bad, but man, I was done with this series. And now I'm actually done with this series, so let's talk about some stuff I liked about it:<br /><u> Dark </u><br />I'm a sucker for randomly inserted characters with zero social skills who end up fixing all the major problems. I know how he ended the book is a little bit of a cop-out, but do I care? No.<br /><br /><u> Renn and Torak </u><br />Seriously dude, been waiting since book one. <br /><br /><u> Being Done </u><br />There's always some sort of awesome quality that the last book in a series has, whether it's good or not. And this wasn't<i> bad</i>. And it definitely had that quality of the Last Book, where everything is heightened and you know it has to be finished up now and that was cool.<br /><br />So that's that. I'm done. I'm done. And Michelle Paver, not being Satan incarnate, is not writing a sequel series so I don't have to read any more. </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/71007746-dyslexic-bookmonster?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/71007746-dyslexic-bookmonster?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2632446813" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4513497244672647397">When I read this story for the first time all those years ago, I did not specifically know (or rather understood) why I was bothered by the way the story was spun. For a long time, I thought I felt this way because the story was ending, a story which I would have liked to never end. <br/>Now I believe that I know better, I understand what bothered me back then and what still bothered me now that I was rereading the book. <br/>In my opinion, all characters, except for Torak, were neglected in their 'develo</span>
  <span id="freeText4513497244672647397" style="display:none">When I read this story for the first time all those years ago, I did not specifically know (or rather understood) why I was bothered by the way the story was spun. For a long time, I thought I felt this way because the story was ending, a story which I would have liked to never end. <br />Now I believe that I know better, I understand what bothered me back then and what still bothered me now that I was rereading the book. <br />In my opinion, all characters, except for Torak, were neglected in their 'development' (for lack of a better word). Not in the usual way, for most (but not all!) the characters were given a cause for their deeds and all the new characters had a background story to fall back on. No, with 'lacking in development' I meant that the characters felt too... well prepared? Lacking in emotional depth? Though I have to admit, Wolf had a rough period during the story. Yet, still, I felt like emotions were missing thorough the book. And especially Eostra had to take the burn for it. She was the epitome of evil, which is not a bad thing on itself, but in this case, she was so... boring.<br />Perhaps the story went too fast; if only it had been given more pages to give depth to the crucial events in the book. Instead, Torak, Wolf and Ren were thrown from one chaos into another.<br /><br />So why am I still giving it four stars? Because... Well... You see... I am guilty of being biased. This series showed me when I was still a mini-me that reading could be fun. And for that, I will always be thankful. </span>
  <a data-text-id="4513497244672647397" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Oddly, I felt like the horror element in this book wasn't as great as</span>
  <span id="freeText10179085249911055084" style="display:none">"The entire series is 5 stars. A little bit like the last book of Harry Potter at the very end" said Tyler, my 8 year-old son.<br /><br />Update 3/28/13:<br />Wow and wow. I loved this book! I tore through it not being able to handle the anticipation of how this journey ended. At the beginning, there are some of those things that do get repetitive - c'mom Torak, would you stop going off by yourself!! It is getting to be like a bad horror movie! Oddly, I felt like the horror element in this book wasn't as great as the others, but that could also be that we knew the evil so well at this point that it is not as much of a shock to encounter it.<br /><br />But Michelle Paver throws in some great twists with the plot that I really appreciated. I don't want to give away any spoilers, so I will simply say that her choices allowed the last part of this journey to be as epic as it should be. And I loved how she handled the ending - I didn't think of it ending the way it did, but it makes perfectly wonderful sense. The possibility was foreshadowed and I hadn't picked up on it.<br /><br />This was also my favorite series. I give props to Ms. Paver for creating a vivid natural world and offering a look at each of the clans and their rituals in great detail.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10179085249911055084" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText18375273781575541182" style="display:none">Wow. I literally read this book in one day. I couldn't put it down because the story is so gripping but at the same time I didn't want the story to end as this is the last book in the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness series and for me that was really sad - some parts of this story genuinely made me tear up especially because over the course of the series you really get to know and care about the characters involved. It doesn't often happen, but when I'd finished the book I really did not know what I would read next that would hold the same amount of sway over my attention and emotions! The last time this happened was with the Harry Potter stories. Michelle Paver is a brilliant writer and story teller for children and adults in equal measure by far matching and surpassing authors such as JK Rowling - It's good to know there's life after Harry Potter for young readers out there and I now know I can confidently recommend Michelle Paver to any student who comes up to me in the library asking for suggestions of the epic variety.<br /><br /></span>

  <span id="freeText1896790048246202473" style="display:none">How I would have loved to have had these books read to me when I was a child, or to follow the 6 books of the series through on my own with as much excitement as I saw in youngsters waiting for the next Harry Potter to come out. Ok SPOILER .......there is a Hollywood ending but it is what you want, Paver tells an exceedingly good tale, and I can only reiterate what I said on others McKellan's reading is just brilliant. It is a standard tale of good v evil but I loved her characters, I loved the mythology of the clans she has invented - the Raven clan, the Seal clan, the Wolf clan the Red Deer clan and others each with their own clan creature, herbology, traditions and spiritualism. The books deserve some serious cgi film making techniques a la Peter Jackson. If you are in the mood for a jolly good storyline, I can't recommend them highly enough.</span>

<div id="review_2460547342" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2460547342" />
    <a title="Emma Larsson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/52012594-emma-larsson"><img alt="Emma Larsson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1455064267p2/52012594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2460547342?book_show_action=true">Jun 01, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emma Larsson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emma Larsson" href="/user/show/52012594-emma-larsson">Emma Larsson</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9789176510438" href="/book/show/45679061-v-lnadernas-berg">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52012594-emma-larsson?shelf=four-stars">four-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52012594-emma-larsson?shelf=read-in-2019">read-in-2019</a>,

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer2460547342&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2460547342" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4714081565469157333">Woah, I'm finished?<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440988683ra/16049298.gif' width='400' height='210' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This series was one of the first I read that was a bit more serious, I even read the first book before I read Harry Potter. It feels a bit weird that it's over, but mostly I feel accomplished. I'm done! This series has been gnawing in the back of my head ever since I started reading books seriously in 2016 again (not because the books are bad, but because it's a series of books I started and never finished) so it feels really wonderful to be done with them.<br/><br/>This last book felt </span>
  <span id="freeText4714081565469157333" style="display:none">Woah, I'm finished?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440988683ra/16049298.gif" width="400" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This series was one of the first I read that was a bit more serious, I even read the first book before I read Harry Potter. It feels a bit weird that it's over, but mostly I feel accomplished. I'm done! This series has been gnawing in the back of my head ever since I started reading books seriously in 2016 again (not because the books are bad, but because it's a series of books I started and never finished) so it feels really wonderful to be done with them.<br><br>This last book felt many times like a cinema manuscript. There were times in the book, especially near the end, where I felt like I was reading notes for how a scene was supposed to look like rather than description in a book. I'm unsure if it's because of Michelle also seeing this in front of her eyes, thinking "oh wow, I need to get this down in the book as good as I can!" or if it's a style that Michelle has dove into and it still trying to figure out how to write in. I sort of like it, because it really gave me amazing visual images in my head, thinking "this would look SO GOOD on cinema" but at the same time it took me a bit out of the story and distanced me a bit from the characters. There were for example more descriptions about how their hands were moving and how everything was placed than their feelings and what was going on inside.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1500049417ra/23294277.gif" width="400" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really like Dark as a character, however I wish he would've gotten introduced before. It really felt like Michelle didn't have the end figured out until this book, and now she wanted Renn to go with Torak, so she had to introduce a new shaman to take her place. Deus ex Dark to your service.<br><br>Speaking of which, the ending was lovely! I would've loved for Renn and Torak to stay though, but it would've felt a bit out of character. This was truly the best thing, and for my own I can see them coming back and visit often, just to not break my heart too much.<br><br>I wrote in the review to the fourth book;<br><br><blockquote>"STILL no romance between these two?? Not even a mention? I'd actually be happy if it turns out they never get together in a romantic way at all and just stay as friends, but if the next book (or god forbid, the last one) suddenly drops the "oh I love him/her" bomb I'm going to be so pissed."</blockquote><br><br>Well, it happened, and I didn't get pissed. I was expecting it, and even though it still felt a bit out of the blue it was cute. They never went from friends to lovers over a night, they have always balanced on that wave and the most intimate thing that happened was that Torak kissed her. They never confessed their love and they never even acknowledge it. It was dealt with very well.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1559398556ra/27602801.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved Wolf's family. I was heartbroken when they disappeared, was as happy when Renn found the female, and very pleased that one of the cubs survived. Suspense, sadness, anger and then happiness. I think the wolves journey was more interesting to me than the humans to be honest.<br><br>I also think it was very sweet of Wolf to guide Torak's soul back to his body. I think it was the most beautiful thing in the whole book, maybe the whole series. I didn't think of it much when I read it/listened to it, but now that I think about it, it's just really sweet. Also the fact that Wolf was laying still on top of him to "stop his spirit from leaving". So cute!!<br><br>Overall, this was a great book, and a great series. I may be a bit too old for it, but I still enjoyed every bit of it. Some of the books were better, some where slower and a bit uninteresting, but I'm glad I read them all. I really love the Stone Age and old civilisations so in that way these books have really helped me to get into their world. Michelle's knowledge and the time she puts into researching everything it really admirable. So thanks, Paver, for these books. I might read some other of your stories one day.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1559398556ra/27602800.gif" width="400" height="190" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="4714081565469157333" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2192090400" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2192090400" />
    <a title="Brittney Tyler" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/56506626-brittney-tyler"><img alt="Brittney Tyler" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2192090400?book_show_action=true">Oct 24, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brittney Tyler" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brittney Tyler" href="/user/show/56506626-brittney-tyler">Brittney Tyler</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780060728403" href="/book/show/7217246-ghost-hunter-chronicles-of-ancient-darkness-6">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Young readers!!!!!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56506626-brittney-tyler?shelf=personal-library">personal-library</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2192090400" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7998518074148689377">Star Rating: 4 stars<br/><br/>Note: This is the 6th book in the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness series so this will not be an in-depth review. <br/><br/>After finding out that Michelle Paver will be continuing the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness series in 2020, I decided to pick up the one book by her that I still hadn’t read, Ghost Hunter. This book chronicles the end of Torak’s journey to save his world from the evil Soul Eaters and to redeem his parent’s names. <br/><br/>The best thing about this book is the message that Pa</span>
  <span id="freeText7998518074148689377" style="display:none">Star Rating: 4 stars<br /><br />Note: This is the 6th book in the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness series so this will not be an in-depth review. <br /><br />After finding out that Michelle Paver will be continuing the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness series in 2020, I decided to pick up the one book by her that I still hadn’t read, Ghost Hunter. This book chronicles the end of Torak’s journey to save his world from the evil Soul Eaters and to redeem his parent’s names. <br /><br />The best thing about this book is the message that Paver is trying to convey. Within the confines of this book, there are two different characters that are very unique and that don’t quite fit in. One is our main character, Torak, and the other is a character that he meets on his journey, Dark. If you have read the series, then you know that Torak has always felt apart from others in this world because of his special abilities and the way he was raised, but Dark was ostracized from society simply because of the way he looks and acts. Dark has albinism and possibly psychic abilities, and because of this his clan thought that he was possessed or cursed so his father abandoned him within a scared gorge, fully expecting him to die. Through these characters and their stories, Paver introduces her readers to the concept of diversity and the fact that everyone is different, some obviously and some not, but that however one is different, it is okay. I think this is a great concept to teach children especially as they enter into school/the world and start meeting new people. <br /><br />I only have one problem with this book and series in general, and that I wish that the reasons for why Torak is the way he is and why he is the only one who can complete these quests was explained a lot earlier in the series. Paver waited to book 5 to start to explain why she was putting Torak through all this pain, and I feel that she should have started addressing the reasons in book 1 and slowly revealed more and more details with each consecutive book as it would have packed a lot more punch instead of leaving the readers confused and questioning why. <br /><br />All in all, this was a great series ender, and I am looking forward to Paver’s 2020 continuation. 4 stars!!!!!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7998518074148689377" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6297690480166581115">Loved this book, obviously! It's such a powerful and incredible finale. The atmosphere from the very beginning presses on you, pushing you forward the same way it pushes Torak to his destiny. <br/><br/>In case I haven't said it already, Torak is one of my favourite characters. And, honestly, now that I think about it, he probably was the forerunner for all of most favourite characters to come – especially Percy from PJO. I mean Renn is even very similar to Annabeth in a lot of ways, even where their relat</span>
  <span id="freeText6297690480166581115" style="display:none">Loved this book, obviously! It's such a powerful and incredible finale. The atmosphere from the very beginning presses on you, pushing you forward the same way it pushes Torak to his destiny. <br /><br />In case I haven't said it already, Torak is one of my favourite characters. And, honestly, now that I think about it, he probably was the forerunner for all of most favourite characters to come – especially Percy from PJO. I mean Renn is even very similar to Annabeth in a lot of ways, even where their relationship is somewhat more dissimilar. The way that Torak and Renn grew together in the three years they knew each other, in that unspoken way of theirs, was unbelievably well done. When he leaves Renn after she hurts her ankle (!!! I just remember being a kid and flipping back to that scene so many times, I was clearly hopelessly into angst even then lol). But when Renn calls him out as he tries to leave her that last time and the way they celebrate with the wolves and ravens (! and before that with Dark in the snow!!!)... I just love them together so much. <br /><br />One more thing to finish off my observations about warnings and whatever. I can't believe Torak's Fa's warning (and that whole storyline really) came back around in this last book by Renn being the one to remind him to "Look behind you!" What a wonderful full circle moment, even though such heartbreak followed. <br /><br />I think I'm going to try to better put together my thoughts on this series in some kind of longer form. I may update my reviews eventually to reflect that? <br /><br />In the meantime, I've also already started the next book (the one that came out in April!!!) and I am so nervous. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6297690480166581115" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_3138639867" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3138639867" />
    <a title="Lili" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/99807487-lili"><img alt="Lili" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1567151649p2/99807487.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3138639867?book_show_action=true">Jan 19, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lili" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lili" href="/user/show/99807487-lili">Lili</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3138639867" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9678713485949747367">This series is good enough that I completed all six books at a run. As a result, this review is more of the entire series than it is of the final book. I enjoyed them greatly and wish they'd existed when I was a young adult. In particular, the "tokoroth" is by far one of the most horrifying concepts I've read about (that may be because I'm a parent, though I hope the horror of such a creature's creation and existence would not be lost on a YA audience). I had many moments throughout the series w</span>
  <span id="freeText9678713485949747367" style="display:none">This series is good enough that I completed all six books at a run. As a result, this review is more of the entire series than it is of the final book. I enjoyed them greatly and wish they'd existed when I was a young adult. In particular, the "tokoroth" is by far one of the most horrifying concepts I've read about (that may be because I'm a parent, though I hope the horror of such a creature's creation and existence would not be lost on a YA audience). I had many moments throughout the series when I felt that these books have a place in the horror genre. However, there are certainly some criticisms to be made. Mainly, I feel that there should have been far more characters- there are only about half a dozen people who have recurring roles, and others are barely mentioned, even though in the time period of these novels, tribal life would have been close-knit and even someone who was brought up away from the tribe would have had many close ties once they joined. Also, character development was in general extremely shallow. I only felt that I came to know three human characters. The others were extremely one-dimensional and their behaviour predictable. However, despite these flaws I was delighted to learn that the series will continue, and I will be reading future books.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9678713485949747367" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3516741238" />
    <a title="Mouthy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/120497078-mouthy"><img alt="Mouthy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598483718p2/120497078.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3516741238?book_show_action=true">Sep 15, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3516741238" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3743648404583891607">Ending any epic series is a struggle. <br/>Over the years or months we, the reader, become invested in the characters and their world. Which in turn would make it hard for any author to make sure the ending lives up to the series reputation. <br/>Ancient Chronicles of Darkness, though classified as Children's Books, are a set of six incredible stories and Ghost Hunter is the final adventure. <br/><br/>Throughout the series each character has gone through hardships and grown as a being. <br/>Within Ghost Hunter there are</span>
  <span id="freeText3743648404583891607" style="display:none">Ending any epic series is a struggle. <br />Over the years or months we, the reader, become invested in the characters and their world. Which in turn would make it hard for any author to make sure the ending lives up to the series reputation. <br />Ancient Chronicles of Darkness, though classified as Children's Books, are a set of six incredible stories and Ghost Hunter is the final adventure. <br /><br />Throughout the series each character has gone through hardships and grown as a being. <br />Within Ghost Hunter there are many traumatic moments that leave you breathless. Paver has an incredible talent for cramming in so much delight and detail into a maximum of 250 pgs, without it being complicated or overwhelming. <br />Up until the very last word you are holding your breath wondering where the storyline is going, are the characters safe and of course, what kind of ending...<br /><br />For a children's series, this is an incredible tale. <br />I am glad I have had a chance to read it as an adult, as it has given me more time to truly appreciate Paver's talent as a storyteller. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3743648404583891607" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('2R8olMTJHzyarTE1qV0SSUDtd1UDVV/x+UWmdDAQ90fH2igVHKXiCKehVw9ni1zMxkEOah01FRxIcM7BDwqZMQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer6826062150436340215">Michelle Paver was born in Central Africa, but came to England as a child. After gaining a degree in Biochemistry from Oxford University, she became a partner in a City law firm, but eventually gave that up to write full-time.<br/><br/>The hugely successful <i>Chronicles of Ancient Darkness</i> series arose from Michelle's lifelong passion for animals, anthropology and the distant past - as as well as an encounter</span>
  <span id="freeText6826062150436340215" style="display:none">Michelle Paver was born in Central Africa, but came to England as a child. After gaining a degree in Biochemistry from Oxford University, she became a partner in a City law firm, but eventually gave that up to write full-time.<br /><br />The hugely successful <i>Chronicles of Ancient Darkness</i> series arose from Michelle's lifelong passion for animals, anthropology and the distant past - as as well as an encounter with a large bear in a remote valley in southern California. To research the books, Michelle has traveled to Finland, Greenland, Sweden, Norway, Arctic Canada and the Carpathian Mountains. She has slept on reindeer skins, swum with wild orca (killer whales), and got nose-to-nose with polar bears - and, of course, wolves. </span>
